<script>
  (() => {
    const header  = document.getElementById('site-header');
    const burger  = document.getElementById('site-burger');
    const mobile  = document.getElementById('site-mobile-nav');
    const input   = document.getElementById('site-search-input');
    const results = document.getElementById('site-search-results');
    const indexEl = document.getElementById('site-search-index');
    if (!header || !input || !results || !indexEl) return;

    /* ── Desktop mega menus: hover opens (CSS); click/tap toggles; Esc closes ─ */
    const groups = [...document.querySelectorAll('[data-group]')];
    const closeGroups = (except) => groups.forEach(g => {
      if (g !== except) { g.classList.remove('open'); g.querySelector('.nav-trigger')?.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false'); }
    });
    groups.forEach(g => {
      const btn = g.querySelector('.nav-trigger');
      btn?.addEventListener('click', e => {
        e.stopPropagation();
        const open = g.classList.toggle('open');
        btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded', String(open));
        closeGroups(g);
      });
    });
    document.addEventListener('click', e => { if (!e.target.closest('[data-group]')) closeGroups(); });

    /* ── Mobile menu toggle ─────────────────────────────── */
    function setMenu(open) {
      burger.setAttribute('aria-expanded', String(open));
      burger.setAttribute('aria-label', open ? 'Close menu' : 'Open menu');
      mobile.hidden = !open;
      header.classList.toggle('open', open);
      document.body.style.overflow = open ? 'hidden' : '';
    }
    burger?.addEventListener('click', () => {
      setMenu(burger.getAttribute('aria-expanded') !== 'true');
    });
    mobile?.addEventListener('click', e => {
      if (e.target.closest('.site-mobile-link')) setMenu(false);
    });
    document.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
      if (e.key === 'Escape') {
        if (burger?.getAttribute('aria-expanded') === 'true') setMenu(false);
        closeGroups();
      }
    });
    window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
      if (window.innerWidth > 920 && burger?.getAttribute('aria-expanded') === 'true') setMenu(false);
    });

    /* ── Search index ───────────────────────────────────── */
    let INDEX = [];
    try { INDEX = JSON.parse(indexEl.textContent || '[]'); } catch {}

    let active = -1;
    let lastMatches = [];

    function score(item, terms) {
      let s = 0;
      for (const t of terms) {
        if (!item.q.includes(t)) return -1;
        if (item.q.startsWith(t)) s += 10;
        else if (item.q.includes(' ' + t)) s += 5;
        else s += 1;
      }
      return s;
    }

    function search(qRaw) {
      const q = qRaw.trim().toLowerCase();
      if (!q) return [];
      const terms = q.split(/\s+/).filter(Boolean);
      const out = [];
      for (const it of INDEX) {
        const sc = score(it, terms);
        if (sc >= 0) out.push({ sc, it });
      }
      out.sort((a, b) => b.sc - a.sc);
      return out.slice(0, 8).map(r => r.it);
    }

    // Empty-state suggestions: a fresh random handful so the dropdown is useful
    // the moment it opens, before the user types anything.
    function featured(n = 8) {
      const pool = INDEX.slice();
      for (let i = pool.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
        const j = (Math.random() * (i + 1)) | 0;
        [pool[i], pool[j]] = [pool[j], pool[i]];
      }
      return pool.slice(0, n);
    }

    // Featured cars when the box is empty, live results once typing starts.
    function refresh() {
      if (input.value.trim()) { lastMatches = search(input.value); render(lastMatches); }
      else { lastMatches = featured(); render(lastMatches, 'Trending cars'); }
    }

    function render(matches, label) {
      if (!matches.length) {
        results.hidden = true;
        results.innerHTML = '';
        active = -1;
        return;
      }
      results.hidden = false;
      const head = label ? `<div class="site-search-head">${escape(label)}</div>` : '';
      results.innerHTML = head + matches.map((it, i) => `
        <a class="site-search-row" role="option" data-i="${i}" href="/cars/${it.s}">
          <img class="site-search-thumb" src="${it.h}" alt="" loading="lazy" />
          <div class="site-search-text">
            <div class="site-search-name">${escape(it.m)}</div>
            <div class="site-search-sub">${it.y} · ${escape(it.k)}</div>
          </div>
          <span class="site-search-pi pi-${(it.c || '').toLowerCase()}">${escape(it.c || '')} · ${it.p}</span>
        </a>
      `).join('');
      active = -1;
    }

    function escape(s) {
      return String(s).replace(/[&<>"']/g, c => ({
        '&': '&amp;', '<': '&lt;', '>': '&gt;', '"': '&quot;', "'": '&#39;',
      })[c]);
    }

    function setActive(i) {
      const rows = results.querySelectorAll('.site-search-row');
      rows.forEach(r => r.removeAttribute('data-active'));
      if (i >= 0 && rows[i]) {
        rows[i].setAttribute('data-active', 'true');
        rows[i].scrollIntoView({ block: 'nearest' });
      }
      active = i;
    }

    input.addEventListener('input', refresh);
    input.addEventListener('focus', () => {
      closeGroups();
      refresh();
    });
    input.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
      if (e.key === 'ArrowDown') {
        e.preventDefault();
        if (!lastMatches.length) return;
        setActive((active + 1) % lastMatches.length);
      } else if (e.key === 'ArrowUp') {
        e.preventDefault();
        if (!lastMatches.length) return;
        setActive(active <= 0 ? lastMatches.length - 1 : active - 1);
      } else if (e.key === 'Enter') {
        const i = active >= 0 ? active : 0;
        const it = lastMatches[i];
        if (it) { e.preventDefault(); location.href = '/cars/' + it.s; }
      } else if (e.key === 'Escape') {
        input.blur();
        results.hidden = true;
      }
    });

    document.addEventListener('click', e => {
      if (!header.contains(e.target)) results.hidden = true;
    });

    document.addEventListener('keydown', e => {
      const tag = (e.target?.tagName || '').toLowerCase();
      const typing = tag === 'input' || tag === 'textarea' || e.target?.isContentEditable;
      if ((e.key === '/' && !typing) ||
          ((e.metaKey || e.ctrlKey) && e.key.toLowerCase() === 'k')) {
        e.preventDefault();
        input.focus();
        input.select();
      }
    });
  })();
</script> <div class="page-body">  <nav class="crumbs" aria-label="Breadcrumb" data-astro-cid-5q4ejucu> <ol data-astro-cid-5q4ejucu> <li data-astro-cid-5q4ejucu> <a href="/" Horizon 6, rated at 936 PI. Power comes from a normally aspirated 6.3L V12 producing 1,036 hp and 665 lb·ft of torque. Drive is sent to the rear wheels through a 7-speed gearbox.</p> <p class="car-about" data-astro-cid-ic7c7kn2>At 2,831 lb it carries about 2.7 lb per horsepower, with a 41% front weight balance, and tops out near 220 mph in stock form. It hails from Italy, and it plays as a rear-wheel drive car. Ultra high end, purpose-built race cars. class="faq-item" data-astro-cid-ic7c7kn2> <summary data-astro-cid-ic7c7kn2>How much does the FXX K cost in Forza Horizon 6?</summary> <p data-astro-cid-ic7c7kn2>4,300,000 CR at the Autoshow.</p>     // Compare widget — reuses the header's search index (#site-search-index),
    // navigates to /compare with this car pre-selected as A and the pick as B.
    (() => {
      const widget = document.querySelector('.compare-widget');
      const indexEl = document.getElementById('site-search-index');
      if (!widget || !indexEl) return;
      const self = widget.dataset.slug;
      const input = widget.querySelector('.compare-widget-input');
      const wrap = widget.querySelector('.compare-widget-wrap');
      const box = widget.querySelector('.compare-widget-results');
      let INDEX = [];
      try { INDEX = JSON.parse(indexEl.textContent || '[]'); } catch {}
      const esc = s => String(s).replace(/[&<>"']/g, c => (
        { '&': '&amp;', '<': '&lt;', '>': '&gt;', '"': '&quot;', "'": '&#39;' }[c]));

      function search(q) {
        q = q.trim().toLowerCase();
        if (!q) return [];
        const terms = q.split(/\s+/).filter(Boolean);
        const out = [];
        for (const it of INDEX) {
          if (it.s === self) continue;
          let sc = 0, ok = true;
          for (const t of terms) {
            if (!it.q.includes(t)) { ok = false; break; }
            sc += it.q.startsWith(t) ? 10 : it.q.includes(' ' + t) ? 5 : 1;
          }
          if (ok) out.push({ sc, it });
        }
        out.sort((a, b) => b.sc - a.sc);
        return out.slice(0, 6).map(r => r.it);
      }

      function place() {
        // Dropdown is position:fixed so it escapes the stat panel's overflow:hidden.
        const r = wrap.getBoundingClientRect();
        box.style.left = r.left + 'px';
        box.style.top = (r.bottom + 6) + 'px';
        box.style.width = r.width + 'px';
      }

      function render(matches) {
        if (!matches.length) { box.hidden = true; box.innerHTML = ''; return; }
        box.hidden = false;
        place();
        box.innerHTML = matches.map(it => `
          <a class="compare-widget-row" role="option" href="/compare?a=${encodeURIComponent(self)}&b=${encodeURIComponent(it.s)}">
            <img class="compare-widget-thumb" src="${it.h}" alt="" loading="lazy" />
            <span class="compare-widget-text">
              <span class="compare-widget-name">${esc(it.m)}</span>
              <span class="compare-widget-yr">${it.y} · ${esc(it.k)}</span>
            </span>
            <span class="compare-widget-pi pi-${(it.c || '').toLowerCase()}">${esc(it.c)} · ${it.p}</span>
          </a>`).join('');
      }

      input.addEventListener('input', () => render(search(input.value)));
      input.addEventListener('focus', () => { if (input.value) render(search(input.value)); });
      document.addEventListener('click', e => { if (!widget.contains(e.target)) box.hidden = true; });
      // Fixed positioning means the list won't follow the input on scroll, so just
      // close it. (Scrolling inside the list itself doesn't fire a window scroll.)
      window.addEventListener('scroll', () => { box.hidden = true; }, { passive: true });
      window.addEventListener('resize', () => { box.hidden = true; });
    })();
  </script> <script type="module" src="/_astro/_slug_.astro_astro_type_script_index_0_lang.DV8mozlZ.js"></script> <script type="module">const c=new Audio;document.querySelectorAll(".audio-btn").forEach(e=>{e.addEventListener("click",()=>{c.src=e.dataset.src,c.currentTime=0,c.play().catch(()=>{})})});</script>    </div>  </body></html>
